pipe</a></li><li><a class="block text-sm border-l-2 pl-4 -ml-px py-1 mb-1 sm:py-0 transition-all border-transparent hover:border-v-border-active hover:font-semibold hover:underline hover:text-black" building</div></div></a><a class="text-button text-center py-1" href="https://ui.tinybird.co/login">Sign In</a></div></div></div></nav></aside><main class="w-full grow pt-6 pb-6 md:pt-8 sm:pb-8 md:max-w-[calc(100%_-var(--sidebar-width))]" data-pagefind-body=""><div class="hidden sm:block relative max-w-7xl mx-auto px-5 md:px-6 "><nav aria-label="Breadcrumb" class="py-4 max-w-4xl md:px-4 mb-2"><ol class="flex items-center text-sm"><li><a class="hover:font-semibold hover:underline hover:text-black" href="/docs/forward/get-started/quickstarts">Home</a></li><li class="flex items-center"><span class="mx-2 text-v-text-3">/</span><a class="hover:font-semibold hover:underline hover:text-black" href="/docs/forward/get-data-in">Ingest data</a></li><li class="flex items-center"><span class="mx-2 text-v-text-3">/</span><a class="hover:font-semibold hover:underline hover:text-black" href="/docs/forward/get-data-in/connectors">Connectors</a></li><li class="flex items-center"><span class="mx-2 text-v-text-3">/</span><a class="hover:font-semibold hover:underline hover:text-black" href="/docs/forward/get-data-in/connectors/kafka">Kafka</a></li><li class="flex items-center"><span class="mx-2 text-v-text-3">/</span><a class="hover:font-semibold hover:underline hover:text-black" href="/docs/forward/get-data-in/connectors/kafka/guides">Guides</a></li><li class="flex items-center"><span class="mx-2 text-v-text-3">/</span><span class="font-semibold">Schema management</span></li></ol></nav></div><div class="relative max-w-7xl mx-auto px-5 md:px-6 xl:grid xl:grid-cols-[1fr_280px]"><div class="max-w-4xl text-body md:px-4 md:pb-20 relative" role="main"><article><div class="flex flex-col sm:flex-row sm:items-center justify-between gap-4 mb-6"><h1 id="schema-management-and-evolution" class="t-h3" data-pagefind-weight="20.0">Schema management and evolution<a class="headerlink" href="#schema-management-and-evolution" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h1><div class="flex-shrink-0 w-auto"><div class="relative inline-block w-auto" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><div class="flex rounded-md overflow-hidden border border-v-border-02 hover:border-v-border-03 transition-colors"><button class="flex items-center gap-1.5 px-3 py-1.5 text-sm transition-colors min-w-[106px] text-v-text-01"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="w-4 h-4 dark:invert-[0.85] dark:brightness-[0.9]"><path d="M14 2H6a2 2 0 0 0-2 2v16a2 2 0 0 0 2 2h12a2 2 0 0 0 2-2V8z"></path><path d="M14 2v6h6M16 13H8M16 17H8M10 9H8"></path></svg><span>Copy as MD</span></button><button class="flex items-center justify-center px-2 py-1.5 text-sm text-v-text-01 border-l border-v-border-02 min-w-[32px]" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" class="w-3 h-3 dark:invert-[0.85] dark:brightness-[0.9]" style="margin-top:-4px;margin-left:-4px"><path fill="currentColor" d="M8.1 11.41 4 6.995 4.745 6 8.1 9.795 11.454 6l.746.994z"></path></svg></button></div></div></div></div><p>This guide covers managing schemas for Kafka messages in Tinybird, including adding and modifying fields, handling nullable types, data type mapping between Kafka and ClickHouse®, and implementing schema evolution strategies.</p><h2 id="prerequisites" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Prerequisites<a class="headerlink" href="#prerequisites" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><ul><li>Understanding of Kafka message formats (JSON, Avro)</li><li>Basic knowledge of ClickHouse® data types</li><li>Access to Schema Registry (if using Avro or JSON Schema)</li></ul><h2 id="supported-serialization-formats" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Supported serialization formats<a class="headerlink" href="#supported-serialization-formats" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Tinybird supports the following serialization formats:</p><ul><li><strong>JSON</strong> (<code>json_without_schema</code>) - Plain JSON messages</li><li><strong>JSON Schema</strong> (<code>json_with_schema</code>) - JSON with Schema Registry</li><li><strong>Avro</strong> (<code>avro</code>) - Avro with Schema Registry</li></ul><h2 id="adding-and-modifying-fields" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Adding and modifying fields<a class="headerlink" href="#adding-and-modifying-fields" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><h3 id="adding-new-fields" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Adding new fields<a class="headerlink" href="#adding-new-fields" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>When adding new fields to your Kafka messages, the key is making them backward compatible. Old messages (without the field) should still work.</p><p><strong>The pattern:</strong></p><ol><li>Update your Data Source schema to include the new field</li><li>Make it nullable if the field may be missing in older messages</li><li>Provide default values in JSONPath expressions if needed</li></ol><p><strong>Example:</strong></p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="datasources/events_updated.datasource">datasources/events_updated.datasource</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SCHEMA &gt;
    `order_id` String `json:$.order_id`,
    `customer_id` String `json:$.customer_id`,
    `order_total` Float64 `json:$.order_total`,
    `payment_method` Nullable(String) `json:$.payment_method`,  -- New field, nullable
    `data` String `json:$`
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Why nullable? Old messages don&#x27;t have <code>payment_method</code>, so it will be <code>null</code>. After all messages include it, you can make it non-nullable if needed.</p><p><strong>For Avro/JSON Schema:</strong></p><ul><li>Add fields as optional (not in <code>required</code> array)</li><li>Provide default values in Schema Registry</li><li>Use nullable types in ClickHouse</li></ul><h3 id="modifying-existing-fields" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Modifying existing fields<a class="headerlink" href="#modifying-existing-fields" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Modifying existing fields requires more care. Some changes are safe, others require migration.</p><p><strong>Safe modifications:</strong></p><ul><li>Adding default values to existing fields</li><li>Making fields nullable (if they weren&#x27;t before)</li><li>Widening types (Int32 → Int64, String → Nullable(String))</li></ul><p><strong>Example of safe modification:</strong></p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">-- Before: String field
`status` String `json:$.status`

-- After: Still String, but with default
`status` String `json:$.status DEFAULT &#x27;pending&#x27;`
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p><strong>Unsafe modifications (require FORWARD_QUERY):</strong></p><ul><li>Changing field types (String → Int32)</li><li>Narrowing types (Int64 → Int32)</li><li>Removing fields</li></ul><p><strong>Example of type change:</strong></p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">-- Before
`count` Int32 `json:$.count`

-- After: Changed to Int64
`count` Int64 `json:$.count`
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Use FORWARD_QUERY to convert existing data:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">FORWARD_QUERY &gt;
    SELECT
        *,
        toInt64(count) as count  -- Convert Int32 to Int64
    FROM previous_datasource
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>This migrates existing data while new messages use the new type.</p><p><strong>Deploying changes:</strong></p><ul><li>Test locally: <code>tb deploy</code></li><li>Deploy to production: <code>tb --cloud deploy</code></li><li>Always test schema changes in development first</li></ul><h2 id="nullable-vs-non-nullable" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Nullable vs non-nullable<a class="headerlink" href="#nullable-vs-non-nullable" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><h3 id="when-to-use-nullable" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">When to use nullable<a class="headerlink" href="#when-to-use-nullable" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Use <code>Nullable()</code> types when:</p><ul><li>Fields may be missing in some messages</li><li>Fields can have <code>null</code> values</li><li>You&#x27;re adding new optional fields</li><li>You want to handle schema evolution gracefully</li></ul><p><strong>Example:</strong></p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SCHEMA &gt;
    `order_id` String `json:$.order_id`,                    -- Required
    `email` Nullable(String) `json:$.email`,              -- Optional
    `preferences` Nullable(String) `json:$.preferences`, -- Optional
    `data` String `json:$`
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="when-to-use-non-nullable" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">When to use non-nullable<a class="headerlink" href="#when-to-use-non-nullable" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Use non-nullable types when:</p><ul><li>Fields are always present in messages</li><li>You want to enforce data quality</li><li>Fields are required for your use case</li></ul><p><strong>Example:</strong></p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SCHEMA &gt;
    `order_id` String `json:$.order_id`,        -- Always present
    `timestamp` DateTime `json:$.timestamp`,  -- Always present
    `event_type` String `json:$.event_type`,  -- Always present
    `data` String `json:$`
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="handling-missing-fields" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Handling missing fields<a class="headerlink" href="#handling-missing-fields" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>If a field might be missing, provide a default value:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">`status` String `json:$.status DEFAULT &#x27;unknown&#x27;`
`count` Int32 `json:$.count DEFAULT 0`
`is_active` UInt8 `json:$.is_active DEFAULT 0`
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Defaults handle missing fields gracefully without requiring nullable types.</p><h2 id="data-type-mapping" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Data type mapping<a class="headerlink" href="#data-type-mapping" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><h3 id="kafka-to-clickhouse-mapping" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Kafka to ClickHouse® mapping<a class="headerlink" href="#kafka-to-clickhouse-mapping" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="max-w-[calc(100%_+_40px)] overflow-auto -mx-5 ps-5 md:max-w-full md:mx-0 md:ps-0"><table><thead><tr><th>Kafka/JSON Type</th><th>ClickHouse Type</th><th>Notes</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><code>string</code></td><td><code>String</code></td><td>Text data</td></tr><tr><td><code>number</code> (integer)</td><td><code>Int32</code>, <code>Int64</code></td><td>Use Int64 for large numbers</td></tr><tr><td><code>number</code> (float)</td><td><code>Float32</code>, <code>Float64</code></td><td>Use Float64 for precision</td></tr><tr><td><code>boolean</code></td><td><code>UInt8</code>, <code>Boolean</code></td><td>0 or 1, or true/false</td></tr><tr><td><code>null</code></td><td><code>Nullable(T)</code></td><td>Wrap in Nullable</td></tr><tr><td><code>array</code></td><td><code>Array(T)</code></td><td>Specify element type</td></tr><tr><td><code>object</code></td><td><code>String</code> (JSON) or <code>Map(K, V)</code></td><td>Store as JSON string or Map</td></tr></tbody></table></div><h3 id="common-type-conversions" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Common type conversions<a class="headerlink" href="#common-type-conversions" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p><strong>String to DateTime:</strong></p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">`timestamp` DateTime `json:$.timestamp`
-- Assumes ISO 8601 format: &quot;2024-01-01T00:00:00Z&quot;
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p><strong>String to number:</strong></p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">`price` Float64 `json:$.price`
-- JSON numbers are automatically converted
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p><strong>Array handling:</strong></p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">`tags` Array(String) `json:$.tags[:]`
-- For JSON arrays of strings
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p><strong>Nested objects:</strong></p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">`metadata` String `json:$.metadata`
-- Store nested object as JSON string, extract later with JSONExtract
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p><strong>Nested fields:</strong></p><p>For nested JSON structures, use JSONPath to extract specific fields:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SCHEMA &gt;
    `customer_id` String `json:$.customer.id`,
    `customer_email` String `json:$.customer.email`,
    `order_data` String `json:$.order.data`,
    `data` String `json:$`
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p><strong>Maps:</strong></p><p>Use Map type for key-value structures:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">`headers` Map(String, String) `json:$.headers`
-- For Kafka headers or metadata maps
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="schema-registry-integration" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Schema Registry integration<a class="headerlink" href="#schema-registry-integration" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><h3 id="avro-schemas" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Avro schemas<a class="headerlink" href="#avro-schemas" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>When using Avro with Schema Registry:</p><ol><li>Register schema in Schema Registry</li><li>Set format to <code>avro</code> in Data Source</li><li>Configure Schema Registry URL in connection</li></ol><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">KAFKA_VALUE_FORMAT avro
KAFKA_SCHEMA_REGISTRY_URL https://registry.example.com
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p><strong>Schema evolution rules:</strong></p><ul><li>Add optional fields (with defaults)</li><li>Remove fields (backward compatible)</li><li>Change field types only if compatible</li><li>Don&#x27;t change required fields to optional without defaults</li></ul><h3 id="json-schema" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">JSON Schema<a class="headerlink" href="#json-schema" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>When using JSON Schema with Schema Registry:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">KAFKA_VALUE_FORMAT json_with_schema
KAFKA_SCHEMA_REGISTRY_URL https://registry.example.com
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p><strong>Best practices:</strong></p><ul><li>Use schema versioning</li><li>Test schema changes in development</li><li>Monitor schema compatibility</li><li>Add new properties without adding them to <code>required</code></li></ul><h2 id="schema-evolution-strategies" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Schema evolution strategies<a class="headerlink" href="#schema-evolution-strategies" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><h3 id="backward-compatibility" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Backward compatibility<a class="headerlink" href="#backward-compatibility" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Ensure schema changes are backward compatible:</p><p><strong>Safe changes:</strong></p><ul><li>Adding optional fields</li><li>Removing fields</li><li>Making fields nullable</li><li>Adding default values</li><li>Widening types (Int32 → Int64)</li></ul><p><strong>Breaking changes:</strong></p><ul><li>Removing required fields</li><li>Changing field types incompatibly</li><li>Renaming fields</li><li>Narrowing types (Int64 → Int32)</li></ul><h3 id="versioning-strategy" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Versioning strategy<a class="headerlink" href="#versioning-strategy" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>For breaking changes, use topic versioning:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">orders-v1
orders-v2
orders-v3
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Create separate Data Sources for each version, then merge in queries if needed. This is safer than trying to migrate in place.</p><h3 id="gradual-rollout" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Gradual rollout<a class="headerlink" href="#gradual-rollout" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>When adding new fields:</p><ol><li>Add new field as nullable in Data Source</li><li>Update producers to include new field</li><li>Monitor for any issues</li><li>Make field required once all messages include it (optional)</li></ol><p>This approach minimizes risk and allows you to roll back if needed.</p><h2 id="monitoring-schema-changes" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Monitoring schema changes<a class="headerlink" href="#monitoring-schema-changes" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><h3 id="detect-schema-mismatches" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Detect schema mismatches<a class="headerlink" href="#detect-schema-mismatches" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Query <code>kafka_ops_log</code> for deserialization errors:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    timestamp,
    datasource_id,
    topic,
    msg,
    count(*) as error_count
FROM tinybird.kafka_ops_log
WHERE msg_type = &#x27;warning&#x27;
  AND msg LIKE &#x27;%schema%&#x27;
  AND timestamp &gt; now() - INTERVAL 1 hour
GROUP BY timestamp, datasource_id, topic, msg
ORDER BY error_count DESC
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>This helps you catch schema evolution issues early.</p><h3 id="monitor-quarantined-messages" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Monitor quarantined messages<a class="headerlink" href="#monitor-quarantined-messages" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Check Quarantine Data Source for schema-related issues:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    timestamp,
    count(*) as quarantined_count
FROM your_datasource_quarantine
WHERE timestamp &gt; now() - INTERVAL 1 hour
GROUP BY timestamp
ORDER BY timestamp DESC
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Quarantined messages often indicate schema mismatches or data quality issues.</p><h2 id="common-pitfalls" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Common pitfalls<a class="headerlink" href="#common-pitfalls" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><h3 id="changing-field-types-incompatibly" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Changing field types incompatibly<a class="headerlink" href="#changing-field-types-incompatibly" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p><strong>Problem:</strong> Changing <code>count</code> from <code>String</code> to <code>Int32</code> breaks old messages.</p><p><strong>Solution:</strong> Use <code>FORWARD_QUERY</code> to convert types, or add a new field and migrate gradually.</p><h3 id="removing-required-fields" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Removing required fields<a class="headerlink" href="#removing-required-fields" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p><strong>Problem:</strong> Removing a field that old messages require causes deserialization failures.</p><p><strong>Solution:</strong> Make the field optional first, wait for all consumers to update, then remove it.</p><h3 id="not-handling-nullable-fields" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Not handling nullable fields<a class="headerlink" href="#not-handling-nullable-fields" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p><strong>Problem:</strong> Adding a new field as non-nullable breaks old messages that don&#x27;t have it.</p><p><strong>Solution:</strong> Always make new fields nullable initially. After all messages include it, you can make it non-nullable.</p><h3 id="ignoring-schema-registry-compatibility" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Ignoring Schema Registry compatibility<a class="headerlink" href="#ignoring-schema-registry-compatibility" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p><strong>Problem:</strong> Schema changes that violate compatibility settings cause failures.</p><p><strong>Solution:</strong> Check your compatibility mode (<code>BACKWARD</code>, <code>FORWARD</code>, <code>FULL</code>) and test schema changes before deploying.</p><h2 id="best-practices" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Best practices<a class="headerlink" href="#best-practices" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><ol><li><strong>Use nullable types</strong> for optional fields</li><li><strong>Provide default values</strong> for missing fields</li><li><strong>Test schema changes</strong> in development first with <code>tb deploy</code></li><li><strong>Deploy to production</strong> using <code>tb --cloud deploy</code> after testing</li><li><strong>Monitor schema evolution</strong> using <code>kafka_ops_log</code></li><li><strong>Use Schema Registry</strong> for Avro and JSON Schema</li><li><strong>Document schema changes</strong> in your team</li><li><strong>Version schemas</strong> for breaking changes</li><li><strong>Keep schemas backward compatible</strong> when possible</li><li><strong>Start with nullable</strong> when adding new fields</li></ol><h2 id="troubleshooting-schema-issues" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Troubleshooting schema issues<a class="headerlink" href="#troubleshooting-schema-issues" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><h3 id="type-conversion-failed" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Type conversion failed<a class="headerlink" href="#type-conversion-failed" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p><strong>Solutions:</strong></p><ol><li>Verify JSONPath expressions match message structure</li><li>Check data types are compatible</li><li>Use type conversion functions if needed</li><li>Make fields nullable if data might be missing</li></ol><h3 id="schema-mismatch" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Schema mismatch<a class="headerlink" href="#schema-mismatch" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p><strong>Solutions:</strong></p><ol><li>Review Quarantine Data Source for actual message format</li><li>Update Data Source schema to match messages</li><li>Check Schema Registry if using Avro/JSON Schema</li><li>Verify schema evolution is backward compatible</li></ol><h3 id="missing-fields" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Missing fields<a class="headerlink" href="#missing-fields" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p><strong>Solutions:</strong></p><ol><li>Make fields nullable</li><li>Provide default values</li><li>Update producers to include required fields</li><li>Handle missing fields in queries</li></ol><h2 id="related-documentation" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Related documentation<a class="headerlink" href="#related-documentation" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><ul><li><a href="/docs/forward/get-data-in/connectors/kafka">Kafka connector documentation</a> - Main setup and configuration guide</li><li><a href="../troubleshooting">Troubleshooting guide</a> - Schema-related error troubleshooting</li><li><a href="/docs/forward/test-and-deploy/evolve-data-source">Evolve Data Sources</a> - Managing schema changes</li><li><a href="/docs/sql-reference/data-types">ClickHouse® data types</a> - Available data types</li></ul></article><div class="flex items-center justify-end h-10" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><div class="italic text-caption"><span>Updated<!-- --> <time dateTime="2025-12-11T19:06:55.000Z">3 months ago</time></span></div></div><nav class="flex justify-between items-stretch gap-2 md:gap-4 mt-4 border-t border-v-border pt-8" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><div class="flex-1 flex items-stretch"><a href="/docs/forward/get-data-in/connectors/kafka/guides/cicd-version-control" class="group flex items-stretch hover:no-underline flex-1"><div class="flex items-center pe-2 md:pe-4"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" class="w-5 h-5 text-v-text-3 rotate-90"><path fill="currentColor" d="M8.1 11.41 4 6.995 4.745 6 8.1 9.795 11.454 6l.746.994z"></path></svg></div><div class="flex-1 flex flex-col justify-center p-2 md:p-4 rounded-lg border border-v-border hover:border-v-border-active hover:bg-v-bg-active"><span class="text-caption text-v-text-3">Previous</span><span class="text-v-link underline md:mt-1 text-body">CI/CD and version control</span></div></a></div><div class="flex-1 flex items-stretch justify-end"><a href="/docs/forward/get-data-in/connectors/kafka/guides/partitioning-strategies" class="group flex items-stretch hover:no-underline flex-1"><div class="flex-1 flex flex-col Schema management and evolution\nmeta:\n  description: Complete guide to managing Kafka message schemas, including adding fields, handling nullable types, data type mapping, and schema evolution strategies.\n---\n\n# Schema management and evolution\n\nThis guide covers managing schemas for Kafka messages in Tinybird, including adding and modifying fields, handling nullable types, data type mapping between Kafka and ClickHouse®, and implementing schema evolution strategies.\n\n## Prerequisites\n\n- Understanding of Kafka message formats (JSON, Avro)\n- Basic knowledge of ClickHouse® data types\n- Access to Schema Registry (if using Avro or JSON Schema)\n\n## Supported serialization formats\n\nTinybird supports the following serialization formats:\n\n- **JSON** (`json_without_schema`) - Plain JSON messages\n- **JSON Schema** (`json_with_schema`) - JSON with Schema Registry\n- **Avro** (`avro`) - Avro with Schema Registry\n\n## Adding and modifying fields\n\n### Adding new fields\n\nWhen adding new fields to your Kafka messages, the key is making them backward compatible. Old messages (without the field) should still work.\n\n**The pattern:**\n\n1. Update your Data Source schema to include the new field\n2. Make it nullable if the field may be missing in older messages\n3. Provide default values in JSONPath expressions if needed\n\n**Example:**\n\n```tb {% title=\"datasources/events_updated.datasource\" %}\nSCHEMA \u003e\n    `order_id` String `json:$.order_id`,\n    `customer_id` String `json:$.customer_id`,\n    `order_total` Float64 `json:$.order_total`,\n    `payment_method` Nullable(String) `json:$.payment_method`,  -- New field, nullable\n    `data` String `json:$`\n```\n\nWhy nullable? Old messages don't have `payment_method`, so it will be `null`. After all messages include it, you can make it non-nullable if needed.\n\n**For Avro/JSON Schema:**\n\n- Add fields as optional (not in `required` array)\n- Provide default values in Schema Registry\n- Use nullable types in ClickHouse\n\n### Modifying existing fields\n\nModifying existing fields requires more care. Some changes are safe, others require migration.\n\n**Safe modifications:**\n\n- Adding default values to existing fields\n- Making fields nullable (if they weren't before)\n- Widening types (Int32 → Int64, String → Nullable(String))\n\n**Example of safe modification:**\n\n```tb\n-- Before: String field\n`status` String `json:$.status`\n\n-- After: Still String, but with default\n`status` String `json:$.status DEFAULT 'pending'`\n```\n\n**Unsafe modifications (require FORWARD_QUERY):**\n\n- Changing field types (String → Int32)\n- Narrowing types (Int64 → Int32)\n- Removing fields\n\n**Example of type change:**\n\n```tb\n-- Before\n`count` Int32 `json:$.count`\n\n-- After: Changed to Int64\n`count` Int64 `json:$.count`\n```\n\nUse FORWARD_QUERY to convert existing data:\n\n```tb\nFORWARD_QUERY \u003e\n    SELECT\n        *,\n        toInt64(count) as count  -- Convert Int32 to Int64\n    FROM previous_datasource\n```\n\nThis migrates existing data while new messages use the new type.\n\n**Deploying changes:**\n\n- Test locally: `tb deploy`\n- Deploy to production: `tb --cloud deploy`\n- Always test schema changes in development first\n\n## Nullable vs non-nullable\n\n### When to use nullable\n\nUse `Nullable()` types when:\n\n- Fields may be missing in some messages\n- Fields can have `null` values\n- You're adding new optional fields\n- You want to handle schema evolution gracefully\n\n**Example:**\n\n```tb\nSCHEMA \u003e\n    `order_id` String `json:$.order_id`,                    -- Required\n    `email` Nullable(String) `json:$.email`,              -- Optional\n    `preferences` Nullable(String) `json:$.preferences`, -- Optional\n    `data` String `json:$`\n```\n\n### When to use non-nullable\n\nUse non-nullable types when:\n\n- Fields are always present in messages\n- You want to enforce data quality\n- Fields are required for your use case\n\n**Example:**\n\n```tb\nSCHEMA \u003e\n    `order_id` String `json:$.order_id`,        -- Always present\n    `timestamp` DateTime `json:$.timestamp`,  -- Always present\n    `event_type` String `json:$.event_type`,  -- Always present\n    `data` String `json:$`\n```\n\n### Handling missing fields\n\nIf a field might be missing, provide a default value:\n\n```tb\n`status` String `json:$.status DEFAULT 'unknown'`\n`count` Int32 `json:$.count DEFAULT 0`\n`is_active` UInt8 `json:$.is_active DEFAULT 0`\n```\n\nDefaults handle missing fields gracefully without requiring nullable types.\n\n## Data type mapping\n\n### Kafka to ClickHouse® mapping\n\n| Kafka/JSON Type | ClickHouse Type | Notes |\n|----------------|-----------------|-------|\n| `string` | `String` | Text data |\n| `number` (integer) | `Int32`, `Int64` | Use Int64 for large numbers |\n| `number` (float) | `Float32`, `Float64` | Use Float64 for precision |\n| `boolean` | `UInt8`, `Boolean` | 0 or 1, or true/false |\n| `null` | `Nullable(T)` | Wrap in Nullable |\n| `array` | `Array(T)` | Specify element type |\n| `object` | `String` (JSON) or `Map(K, V)` | Store as JSON string or Map |\n\n### Common type conversions\n\n**String to DateTime:**\n\n```tb\n`timestamp` DateTime `json:$.timestamp`\n-- Assumes ISO 8601 format: \"2024-01-01T00:00:00Z\"\n```\n\n**String to number:**\n\n```tb\n`price` Float64 `json:$.price`\n-- JSON numbers are automatically converted\n```\n\n**Array handling:**\n\n```tb\n`tags` Array(String) `json:$.tags[:]`\n-- For JSON arrays of strings\n```\n\n**Nested objects:**\n\n```tb\n`metadata` String `json:$.metadata`\n-- Store nested object as JSON string, extract later with JSONExtract\n```\n\n**Nested fields:**\n\nFor nested JSON structures, use JSONPath to extract specific fields:\n\n```tb\nSCHEMA \u003e\n    `customer_id` String `json:$.customer.id`,\n    `customer_email` String `json:$.customer.email`,\n    `order_data` String `json:$.order.data`,\n    `data` String `json:$`\n```\n\n**Maps:**\n\nUse Map type for key-value structures:\n\n```tb\n`headers` Map(String, String) `json:$.headers`\n-- For Kafka headers or metadata maps\n```\n\n## Schema Registry integration\n\n### Avro schemas\n\nWhen using Avro with Schema Registry:\n\n1. Register schema in Schema Registry\n2. Set format to `avro` in Data Source\n3. Configure Schema Registry URL in connection\n\n```tb\nKAFKA_VALUE_FORMAT avro\nKAFKA_SCHEMA_REGISTRY_URL https://registry.example.com\n```\n\n**Schema evolution rules:**\n\n- Add optional fields (with defaults)\n- Remove fields (backward compatible)\n- Change field types only if compatible\n- Don't change required fields to optional without defaults\n\n### JSON Schema\n\nWhen using JSON Schema with Schema Registry:\n\n```tb\nKAFKA_VALUE_FORMAT json_with_schema\nKAFKA_SCHEMA_REGISTRY_URL https://registry.example.com\n```\n\n**Best practices:**\n\n- Use schema versioning\n- Test schema changes in development\n- Monitor schema compatibility\n- Add new properties without adding them to `required`\n\n## Schema evolution strategies\n\n### Backward compatibility\n\nEnsure schema changes are backward compatible:\n\n**Safe changes:**\n\n- Adding optional fields\n- Removing fields\n- Making fields nullable\n- Adding default values\n- Widening types (Int32 → Int64)\n\n**Breaking changes:**\n\n- Removing required fields\n- Changing field types incompatibly\n- Renaming fields\n- Narrowing types (Int64 → Int32)\n\n### Versioning strategy\n\nFor breaking changes, use topic versioning:\n\n```\norders-v1\norders-v2\norders-v3\n```\n\nCreate separate Data Sources for each version, then merge in queries if needed. This is safer than trying to migrate in place.\n\n### Gradual rollout\n\nWhen adding new fields:\n\n1. Add new field as nullable in Data Source\n2. Update producers to include new field\n3. Monitor for any issues\n4. Make field required once all messages include it (optional)\n\nThis approach minimizes risk and allows you to roll back if needed.\n\n## Monitoring schema changes\n\n### Detect schema mismatches\n\nQuery `kafka_ops_log` for deserialization errors:\n\n```sql\nSELECT\n    timestamp,\n    datasource_id,\n    topic,\n    msg,\n    count(*) as error_count\nFROM tinybird.kafka_ops_log\nWHERE msg_type = 'warning'\n  AND msg LIKE '%schema%'\n  AND timestamp \u003e now() - INTERVAL 1 hour\nGROUP BY timestamp, datasource_id, topic, msg\nORDER BY error_count DESC\n```\n\nThis helps you catch schema evolution issues early.\n\n### Monitor quarantined messages\n\nCheck Quarantine Data Source for schema-related issues:\n\n```sql\nSELECT\n    timestamp,\n    count(*) as quarantined_count\nFROM your_datasource_quarantine\nWHERE timestamp \u003e now() - INTERVAL 1 hour\nGROUP BY timestamp\nORDER BY timestamp DESC\n```\n\nQuarantined messages often indicate schema mismatches or data quality issues.\n\n## Common pitfalls\n\n### Changing field types incompatibly\n\n**Problem:** Changing `count` from `String` to `Int32` breaks old messages.\n\n**Solution:** Use `FORWARD_QUERY` to convert types, or add a new field and migrate gradually.\n\n### Removing required fields\n\n**Problem:** Removing a field that old messages require causes deserialization failures.\n\n**Solution:** Make the field optional first, wait for all consumers to update, then remove it.\n\n### Not handling nullable fields\n\n**Problem:** Adding a new field as non-nullable breaks old messages that don't have it.\n\n**Solution:** Always make new fields nullable initially. After all messages include it, you can make it non-nullable.\n\n### Ignoring Schema Registry compatibility\n\n**Problem:** Schema changes that violate compatibility settings cause failures.\n\n**Solution:** Check your compatibility mode (`BACKWARD`, `FORWARD`, `FULL`) and test schema changes before deploying.\n\n## Best practices\n\n1. **Use nullable types** for optional fields\n2. **Provide default values** for missing fields\n3. **Test schema changes** in development first with `tb deploy`\n4. **Deploy to production** using `tb --cloud deploy` after testing\n5. **Monitor schema evolution** using `kafka_ops_log`\n6. **Use Schema Registry** for Avro and JSON Schema\n7. **Document schema changes** in your team\n8. **Version schemas** for breaking changes\n9. **Keep schemas backward compatible** when possible\n10. **Start with nullable** when adding new fields\n\n## Troubleshooting schema issues\n\n### Type conversion failed\n\n**Solutions:**\n\n1. Verify JSONPath expressions match message structure\n2. Check data types are compatible\n3. Use type conversion functions if needed\n4. Make fields nullable if data might be missing\n\n### Schema mismatch\n\n**Solutions:**\n\n1. Review Quarantine Data Source for actual message format\n2. Update Data Source schema to match messages\n3. Check Schema Registry if using Avro/JSON Schema\n4. Verify schema evolution is backward compatible\n\n### Missing fields\n\n**Solutions:**\n\n1. Make fields nullable\n2. Provide default values\n3. Update producers to include required fields\n4. Handle missing fields in queries\n\n## Related documentation\n\n- [Kafka connector documentation](/forward/get-data-in/connectors/kafka) - Main setup and configuration guide\n- [Troubleshooting guide](../troubleshooting) - Schema-related error troubleshooting\n- [Evolve Data Sources](/forward/test-and-deploy/evolve-data-source) - Managing schema changes\n- [ClickHouse® data types](/sql-reference/data-types) - Available data types\n"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"8:[\"$\",\"div\",null,{\"className\":\"relative max-w-7xl mx-auto px-5 md:px-6 xl:grid xl:grid-cols-[1fr_280px]\",\"children\":[[\"$\",\"div\",null,{\"className\":\"max-w-4xl text-body md:px-4 md:pb-20 relative\",\"role\":\"main\",\"children\":[[\"$\",\"$L20\",null,{\"pageContent\":\"$21\",\"pagePath\":\"forward/get-data-in/connectors/kafka/guides/schema-management\",\"children\":[\"$\",\"article\",null,{\"children\":[[\"$\",\"$L22\",null,{\"level\":1,\"name\":\"Heading\",\"children\":\"Schema management and evolution\"}],[\"$\",\"p\",null,{\"children\":\"This guide covers managing schemas for Kafka messages in Tinybird, including adding and modifying fields, handling nullable types, data type mapping between Kafka and ClickHouse®, and implementing schema evolution strategies.\"}],[\"$\",\"$L22\",null,{\"level\":2,\"name\":\"Heading\",\"children\":\"Prerequisites\"}],[\"$\",\"ul\",null,{\"children\":[[\"$\",\"li\",null,{\"children\":\"Understanding of Kafka message formats (JSON, Avro)\"}],[\"$\",\"li\",null,{\"children\":\"Basic knowledge of ClickHouse® data types\"}],[\"$\",\"li\",null,{\"children\":\"Access to Schema Registry (if using Avro or JSON Schema)\"}]]}],[\"$\",\"$L22\",null,{\"level\":2,\"name\":\"Heading\",\"children\":\"Supported serialization formats\"}],[\"$\",\"p\",null,{\"children\":\"Tinybird supports the following serialization formats:\"}],[\"$\",\"ul\",null,{\"children\":[[\"$\",\"li\",null,{\"children\":[[\"$\",\"strong\",null,{\"children\":\"JSON\"}],\" (\",[\"$\",\"code\",null,{\"children\":\"json_without_schema\"}],\") -
